                    file=sys.stderr,\n                    )\n                    _timed_out = True\n                    proc_manager.terminate()\n                    break\n                else:\n                    # warn action: log and continue\n                    import sys\n                    print(\n                        f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n only fires after some output/events exist: `ms.events_received > 0`\n- it is single-fire per stall episode via `_stall_acted`\n- guard resets only when output resumes and `ms.stall_seconds == 0.0`\n- `\"kill\"` sets `_timed_out = True`, terminates process, breaks loop\n- `\"warn\"` only prints to stderr and continues\n\n## How phases are iterated and halt propagates\n\nPhase iteration is in `execute_sprint(config)`:\n\n- `for phase in config.active_phases:`\n- `SprintConfig.active_phases` is defined in `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/sprint/models.py`:\n  ```python\n  @property\n  def active_phases(self) -> list[Phase]:\n      end = self.end_phase or max(p.number for p in self.phases)\n      return [p for p in self.phases if self.start_phase <= p.number <= end]\n  ```\n\nExecution flow per phase:\n1. pre-loop interrupt check:\n   ```python\n   if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n       sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n       break\n   ```\n2. reset and start `OutputMonitor`\n3. optionally update tmux tail pane\n4. construct `ClaudeProcess(config, phase)` and `start()`\n5. poll until subprocess exits / timeout / interrupt / watchdog kill\n6. determine `exit_code`\n7. if interrupted during poll loop:\n   - write interrupt log\n   - `sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED`\n   - `break`\n8. call `_determine_phase_status(...)`\n9. build `PhaseResult` and append to `sprint_result.phase_results`\n10. if `status.is_failure`:\n    - run diagnostics\n    - `sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.HALTED`\n    - `sprint_result.halt_phase = phase.number`\n    - `break`\n\nHalt propagation details:\n- failure statuses are defined in `PhaseStatus.is_failure`:\n  ```python\n  return self in (PhaseStatus.HALT, PhaseStatus.TIMEOUT, PhaseStatus.ERROR)\n  ```\n- once a phase fails, executor stops iterating immediately\n- later phases are not launched\n- final sprint outcome becomes `SprintOutcome.HALTED`\n- resume location is `halt_phase`\n\n`_determine_phase_status(...)` rules:\n- `124 -> TIMEOUT`\n- nonzero exit -> `ERROR`\n- result file:\n  - `EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT -> HALT`\n  - `EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE -> PASS`\n  - `status: PASS -> PASS`\n  - `status: FAIL/FAILED/FAILURE -> HALT`\n  - `status: PARTIAL -> HALT`\n  - otherwise `PASS_NO_SIGNAL`\n- no result but output exists -> `PASS_NO_REPORT`\n- neither -> `ERROR`\n\nImportant nuance:\n- if both CONTINUE and HALT appear, HALT wins because executor checks `has_halt` first.\n\n## TUI, OutputMonitor, tmux integration points\n\n### TUI integration\nImports in executor:\n```python\nfrom .tui import SprintTUI\nfrom .models import MonitorState\n```\n\nUsage in executor:\n- created once:\n  ```python\n  tui = SprintTUI(config)\n  tui.start()\n  ```\n- initial per-phase update:\n  ```python\n  tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n  ```\n- during poll loop:\n  ```python\n  tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n  ```\n- after phase completion:\n  ```python\n  tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, None)\n  ```\n- final render:\n  ```python\n  tui.update(sprint_result, MonitorState(), None)\n  ```\n- cleanup:\n  ```python\n  tui.stop()\n  ```\n\nTUI behavior is in `start(self) -> Live`\n  - `stop(self)`\n  - `update(self, sprint_result: SprintResult, monitor_state: MonitorState, current_phase: Optional[Phase])`\n- rendering helpers:\n  - `_render(self) -> Panel`\n  - `_build_header(self) -> Text`\n  - `_build_phase_table(self) -> Table`\n  - `_build_progress(self) -> Progress`\n  - `_build_active_panel(self) -> Panel`\n  - `_build_terminal_panel(self) -> Panel`\n\nNotable TUI semantics:\n- shows `RUNNING` if `current_phase` is active and not terminal\n- uses `monitor_state.stall_status` in active panel\n- catches live render errors and sets `_live_failed = True`\n\n### OutputMonitor integration\nImports in executor:\n```python\nfrom .monitor import OutputMonitor\n```\n\nUsage:\n- executor instantiates once with dummy path:\n  ```python\n propagates\n\nPhase iteration is in `execute_sprint(config)`:\n\n- `for phase in config.active_phases:`\n- `SprintConfig.active_phases` is defined in `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/sprint/models.py`:\n  ```python\n  @property\n  def active_phases(self) -> list[Phase]:\n      end = self.end_phase or max(p.number for p in self.phases)\n      return [p for p in self.phases if self.start_phase <= p.number <= end]\n  ```\n\nExecution flow per phase:\n1. pre-loop interrupt check:\n   ```python\n   if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n       sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n       break\n   ```\n2. reset and start `OutputMonitor`\n3. optionally update tmux tail pane\n4. construct `ClaudeProcess(config, phase)` and `start()`\n5. poll until subprocess exits / timeout / interrupt / watchdog kill\n6. determine `exit_code`\n7. if interrupted during poll loop:\n   - write interrupt log\n   - `sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED`\n   - `break`\n8. call `_determine_phase_status(...)`\n9. build `PhaseResult` and append to `sprint_result.phase_results`\n10. if `status.is_failure`:\n    - run diagnostics\n    - `sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.HALTED`\n    - `sprint_result.halt_phase = phase.number`\n    - `break`\n\nHalt propagation details:\n- failure statuses are defined in `PhaseStatus.is_failure`:\n  ```python\n  return self in (PhaseStatus.HALT, PhaseStatus.TIMEOUT, PhaseStatus.ERROR)\n  ```\n- once a phase fails, executor stops iterating immediately\n- later phases are not launched\n- final sprint outcome becomes `SprintOutcome.HALTED`\n- resume location is `halt_phase`\n\n`_determine_phase_status(...)` rules:\n- `124 -> TIMEOUT`\n- nonzero exit -> `ERROR`\n- result file:\n  - `EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT -> HALT`\n  - `EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE -> PASS`\n  - `status: PASS -> PASS`\n  - `status: FAIL/FAILED/FAILURE -> HALT`\n  - `status: PARTIAL -> HALT`\n  - otherwise `PASS_NO_SIGNAL`\n- no result but output exists -> `PASS_NO_REPORT`\n- neither -> `ERROR`\n\nImportant nuance:\n- if both CONTINUE and HALT appear, HALT wins because executor checks `has_halt` first.\n\n## TUI, OutputMonitor, tmux integration points\n\n### TUI integration\nImports in executor:\n```python\nfrom .tui import SprintTUI\nfrom Reset single-fire guard when output resumes\n   161→                if _stall_acted and ms.stall_seconds == 0.0:\n   162→                    _stall_acted = False\n   163→\n   164→                # Update TUI at ~2 Hz (monitor thread handles data extraction)\n   165→                # Wrap in try/except so a display glitch cannot abort the sprint\n   166→                try:\n   167→                    tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n   168→                except Exception as _tui_exc:\n   169→                    import sys\n   170→                    print(f\"[TUI] Display error (continuing sprint): {_tui_exc}\", file=sys.stderr)\n   171→                time.sleep(0.5)\n   172→\n   173→            # Safely read exit code: returncode may be None if terminate raced.\n   174→            # Use _timed_out flag instead of assigning directly to returncode.\n   175→            raw_rc = proc_manager._process.returncode\n   176→            if _timed_out:\n   177→                exit_code = 124\n   178→            else:\n   179→                exit_code = raw_rc if raw_rc is not None else -1\n   180→            monitor.stop()\n   181→            finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   182→            _phase_dur = (finished_at - started_at).total_seconds()\n   183→            debug_log(\n   184→                _dbg,\n   185→                \"PHASE_END\",\n   186→                phase=phase.number,\n   187→                exit_code=exit_code,\n   188→                duration=round(_phase_dur, 1),\n   189→            )\n   190→\n   191→            # Ensure monitor thread and subprocess are cleaned up even on exception.\n   277→        # Each step is independent so one failure does not prevent others.\n   278→        try:\n   279→            monitor.stop()\n   280→        except Exception:\n   281→            pass\n   282→        if proc_manager is not None:\n   283→            try:\n   284→                proc_manager.terminate()\n   285→            except Exception:\n   286→                pass\n   287→        try:\n   288→            tui.stop()\n   289→        except Exception:\n   290→            pass\n   291→        try:\n   292→            signal_handler.uninstall()\n   293→        except Exception:\n   294→            pass\n   295→\n   296→    # Write sentinel exit code file so tmux caller can read the outcome\n   297→    _exitcode = 0 if sprint_result.outcome == SprintOutcome.SUCCESS else 1\n   298→    try:\n   299→        (config.release_dir / \".sprint-exitcode\").write_text(str(_exitcode))\n   300→    except OSError:\n   301→        pass  # best-effort; do not mask the real exit\n   302→\n   303→    if _exitcode != 0:\n   304→        raise SystemExit(_exitcode)\n   305→\n   306→\n   307→def _determine_phase_status(\n   308→    exit_code: int,\n   309→    result_file: Path,\n   310→    output_file: Path,\n   311→) -> PhaseStatus:\n   312→    \"\"\"Parse result file and exit code to determine phase status.\n   313→\n   314→    Priority:\n   315→    1. Timeout (exit 124) -> TIMEOUT\n   316→    2. Non-zero exit -> ERROR\n   317→    3. Result file with EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT -> HALT\n   318→    4. Result file with EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE -> PASS\n   319→    5. Result file with status: PASS/FAIL -> PASS/HALT\n   320→    6. No result file but output exists -> PASS_NO_REPORT\n   321→    7. Launch claude -p subprocess\n    2. Start output monitor thread\n    3. Update TUI in a polling loop until process exits (with timeout)\n    4. Parse result file for CONTINUE/HALT\n    5. Reset monitor for this phase\n            output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n            monitor.reset(output_path)\n            monitor.start()\n\n            # Update tmux tail pane if running in tmux\n            if config.tmux_session_name:\n                update_tail_pane(config.tmux_session_name, output_path)\n\n            # Launch claude\n            proc_manager = ClaudeProcess(config, phase)\n            proc_manager.start()\n            started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n            # Use monotonic clock for deadline enforcement to be immune to NTP adjustments\n            deadline = time.monotonic() + proc_manager.timeout_seconds\n            logger.write_phase_start(phase, started_at)\n\n            debug_log(_dbg, \"PHASE_BEGIN\", phase=phase.number, file=str(phase.file))\n\n            tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n\n            # Poll loop: wait for process to finish while updating TUI\n            # Enforces monotonic timeout via deadline check.\n            _timed_out = False\n            _stall_acted = False  # single-fire guard for watchdog\n            _poll_start = time.monotonic()\n            while proc_manager._process.poll() is None:\n                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                    proc_manager.terminate()\n                    break\n                if time.monotonic() > deadline:\n                    # Timeout reached: kill the process, exit loop\n                    _timed_out = True\n                    proc_manager.terminate()\n                    break\n\n                ms = monitor.state\n                _elapsed = time.monotonic() - _poll_start\n\n                debug_log(\n                    _dbg,\n                    \"poll_tick\",\n                    phase=phase.number,\n                    pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\n                    poll_result=\"running\",\n                    elapsed=round(_elapsed, 1),\n                    output_bytes=ms.output_bytes,\n                    growth_rate=round(ms.growth_rate_bps, 1),\n                    stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\n                    stall_status=ms.stall_status,\n                )\n\n                # --- Watchdog: stall timeout check ---\n                if (\n                    config.stall_timeout > 0\n                    and ms.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout\n                    and ms.events_received > 0  # don't trigger during startup\n                    and not _stall_acted\n                ):\n                    _stall_acted = True\n                    debug_log(\n                        _dbg,\n                        \"watchdog_triggered\",\n                        phase=phase.number,\n                        action=config.stall_action,\n                        stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\n                        pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\n                    )\n                    if config.stall_action == \"kill\":\n                        import sys\n                        print(\n                            f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n                            f\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — killing phase {phase.number}\",\n                            file=sys.stderr,\n                        )\n                        _timed_out = True\n                        proc_manager.terminate()\n                        break\n                    else:\n                        # warn action: log and continue\n                        import sys\n                        print(\n                            f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n                            f\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — warning for phase {phase.number}\",\n                            file=sys.stderr,\n                        )\n\n                # Reset single-fire guard when output resumes\n                if _stall_acted and ms.stall_seconds == 0.0:\n                    _stall_acted = False\n\n                # Update TUI at ~2 Hz (monitor thread handles data extraction)\n                # Wrap in try/except so a display glitch cannot abort the sprint\n                try:\n                    tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n                except Exception as _tui_exc:\n                    import sys\n                    print(f\"[TUI] Display error (continuing sprint): {_tui_exc}\", file=sys.stderr)\n                time.sleep(0.5)\n\n            # best-effort; do not mask the real exit\n\n    if _exitcode != 0:\n        raise SystemExit(_exitcode)\n\n\ndef _determine_phase_status(\n    exit_code: int,\n    result_file: Path,\n    output_file: Path,\n) -> PhaseStatus:\n    \"\"\"Parse result file and exit code to determine phase status.\n\n    Priority:\n    1. Timeout (exit 124) -> TIMEOUT\n    2. Non-zero exit -> ERROR\n    3. Result file with EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT -> HALT\n    4. Result file with EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE -> PASS\n    5. Result file with status: PASS/FAIL -> PASS/HALT\n    6. No result file but output exists -> PASS_NO_REPORT\n    7. No result file and no output -> ERROR\n    \"\"\"\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return PhaseStatus.TIMEOUT\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return PhaseStatus.ERROR\n\n    if result_file.exists():\n        content = result_file.read_text(errors=\"replace\")\n        # Use case-insensitive search for EXIT_RECOMMENDATION tokens to handle\n        # model output that varies in casing. When both CONTINUE and HALT appear\n        # (conflicting signals), HALT wins — the stronger/safer outcome.\n        upper = content.upper()\n        has_continue = \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in upper\n        has_halt = \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in upper\n        if has_halt:\n            return PhaseStatus.HALT\n        if has_continue:\n            return PhaseStatus.PASS\n        if re.search(r\"status:\\s*PASS\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n            return PhaseStatus.PASS\n        if re.search(r\"status:\\s*FAIL(?:ED|URE)?\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n            return PhaseStatus.HALT\n        # PARTIAL result means tasks did not fully complete — treat as halt\n        if re.search(r\"status:\\s*PARTIAL\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n            return PhaseStatus.HALT\n        return PhaseStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n\n    if output_file.exists() and output_file.stat().st_size > 0:\n        return PhaseStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT\n\n    return PhaseStatus.ERROR\n","numLines":353,"startLine":1,"totalLines":353}}}
